+# AI Workflow Developer - Curriculum Design Demo Inputs
+
+## Overview
+This document contains all the input fields needed to demo the curriculum design platform (P1-P5 phases) for the **AI Workflow Developer** role.
+
+---
+
+## P1: Purpose Generator
+
+### Basic Information
+| Field | Value |
+|-------|-------|
+| **Job Role** | AI Workflow Developer |
+| **Industry** | Infocomm Technology |
+| **Track** | Artificial Intelligence |
+
+### Purpose Statement Components
+
+**Target Audience:**
+```
+Mid-level developers and data professionals transitioning into AI workflow development roles
+```
+
+**Learning Goals:**
+```
+Design, build, and deploy production-ready AI workflows using modern orchestration frameworks, integrate LLMs with enterprise systems, and implement robust monitoring and evaluation pipelines
+```
+
+**Business Outcomes:**
+```
+Reduce AI solution deployment time by 50%, improve model reliability through systematic evaluation, and enable scalable AI-powered automation across business processes
+```
+
+**Time Frame:**
+```
+Within six months
+```
+
+### Course Learning Outcomes (CLOs)
+
+| # | CLO Statement | Bloom's Level |
+|---|---------------|---------------|
+| 1 | Analyze business requirements to identify suitable AI workflow patterns and architectures | L4 - Analyze |
+| 2 | Design multi-agent AI systems using orchestration frameworks like LangGraph, CrewAI, or AutoGen | L6 - Create |
+| 3 | Implement RAG (Retrieval-Augmented Generation) pipelines with vector databases and embedding models | L3 - Apply |
+| 4 | Evaluate AI workflow performance using systematic testing and observability tools | L5 - Evaluate |
+| 5 | Integrate LLM-powered workflows with enterprise APIs, databases, and external services | L3 - Apply |
+| 6 | Deploy and monitor AI workflows in production environments with proper error handling and fallback strategies | L3 - Apply |
+
+---
+
+## P2: Skills & Competencies Analyzer
+
+### Singapore Skills Framework Search
+| Field | Value |
+|-------|-------|
+| **Search Term** | "Artificial Intelligence" or "Machine Learning" |
+| **Sector** | Infocomm Technology |
+| **Track** | Artificial Intelligence |
+| **Job Role** | AI Engineer / Machine Learning Engineer |
+
+### Selected TSCs (Technical Skills & Competencies)
+
+| TSC Code | Title | Level |
+|----------|-------|-------|
+| ICT-DTA-5001-1.1 | Machine Learning | 5 |
+| ICT-DTA-5002-1.1 | Deep Learning | 5 |
+| ICT-DTA-4003-1.1 | Natural Language Processing | 4 |
+| ICT-SWD-5012-1.1 | Software Design | 5 |
+
+### Additional Context
+
+**Industry Context:**
+```
+Enterprise AI, Generative AI Applications, AI-powered Automation, LLMOps
+```
+
+**Career Level:**
+```
+Mid-level, Senior, Lead AI Developer
+```
+
+---
+
+## P3: Subject Matter Extractor
+
+### Scope Boundary
+
+**Domain Scope:**
+```
+AI workflow development encompasses the design, implementation, and deployment of production-grade AI systems that orchestrate multiple AI components, integrate with enterprise systems, and deliver reliable automated solutions. Focus areas include LLM orchestration, multi-agent systems, RAG architectures, and AI observability.
+```
+
+### Inclusion/Exclusion Criteria
+
+**Include:**
+```
+- LLM orchestration frameworks (LangChain, LangGraph, LlamaIndex)
+- Multi-agent system design (CrewAI, AutoGen, custom agents)
+- RAG pipeline implementation (vector databases, embeddings, retrieval strategies)
+- Prompt engineering and optimization
+- AI workflow testing and evaluation (LangSmith, Weights & Biases)
+- Production deployment patterns (streaming, async, batch)
+- Error handling and fallback strategies
+- Integration patterns with APIs and databases
+```
+
+**Exclude:**
+```
+- Model training and fine-tuning from scratch
+- Deep learning architecture design
+- Data engineering and ETL pipelines
+- Frontend/UI development
+- Basic Python programming fundamentals
+- Cloud infrastructure management (DevOps focus)
+```
+
+### Depth & Breadth Specifications
+
+**Depth Level:**
+```
+Advanced application with emphasis on production-ready implementations. Learners should be able to architect and build complete AI workflow solutions independently.
+```
+
+**Breadth Coverage:**
+```
+Comprehensive coverage of modern AI orchestration ecosystem with practical focus on 3-4 major frameworks and their integration patterns.
+```
+
+**Bloom's Taxonomy Distribution:**
+| Level | Percentage | Focus Areas |
+|-------|------------|-------------|
+| L2 - Understand | 10% | Core concepts, terminology, architecture patterns |
+| L3 - Apply | 40% | Implementation, integration, deployment |
+| L4 - Analyze | 20% | Requirements analysis, debugging, optimization |
+| L5 - Evaluate | 15% | Testing, benchmarking, quality assessment |
+| L6 - Create | 15% | System design, novel solutions, architecture |
+
+---
+
+## P4: Learner Profile Analyzer
+
+### Target Audience Demographics
+
+**Primary Target Roles:**
+```
+Software Developer, Backend Engineer, Data Scientist, ML Engineer, Solutions Architect
+```
+
+**Seniority Level:**
+```
+Mid-level to Senior (3-8 years experience)
+```
+
+**Industry Background:**
+```
+Technology, FinTech, Healthcare Tech, E-commerce, Enterprise Software, Consulting
+```
+
+**Educational Background:**
+```
+Bachelor's or Master's degree in Computer Science, Software Engineering, Data Science, or related technical fields
+```
+
+### Learning Preferences
+
+**Available Study Time:**
+```
+8-12 hours per week
+```
+
+**Preferred Learning Mode:**
+```
+Blended (online self-paced + live workshops)
+```
+
+**Technology Access:**
+```
+- Personal laptop with GPU (optional) or cloud GPU access
+- Python development environment (VS Code, PyCharm)
+- API access to LLM providers (OpenAI, Anthropic, etc.)
+- Cloud platform access (AWS, GCP, or Azure)
+- Git and version control tools
+- Docker for containerization
+```
+
+### Prior Knowledge & Experience
+
+**Required Prerequisites:**
+```
+- Proficient in Python programming (3+ years)
+- Experience with REST APIs and web services
+- Basic understanding of machine learning concepts
+- Familiarity with Git version control
+- Experience with at least one cloud platform
+```
+
+**Experience Level with AI/ML:**
+```
+Intermediate - Has worked with ML models but limited experience with LLMs and AI orchestration
+```
+
+**Motivation:**
+```
+Career advancement into AI-focused roles, building production AI systems, staying current with generative AI developments
+```
+
+---
+
